31  import java.nio.charset.Charset;
32  import java.nio.charset.CharsetDecoder;
33  import java.nio.charset.CharsetEncoder;
34  import java.nio.charset.CharacterCodingException;
35  import sun.nio.cs.HistoricallyNamedCharset;
36  import sun.nio.cs.ext.*;
37  
38  
39  public class IBM935_OLD extends Charset implements HistoricallyNamedCharset
40  {
41  
42      public IBM935_OLD() {
43          super("x-IBM935_Old", null);
44      }
45  
46      public String historicalName() {
47          return "Cp935";
48      }
49  
50      public boolean contains(Charset cs) {
51          return (cs instanceof IBM935);
52      }
53  
54      public CharsetDecoder newDecoder() {
55          return new Decoder(this);
56      }
57  
58      public CharsetEncoder newEncoder() {
59          return new Encoder(this);
60      }
61  
62  
63      /**
64       * These accessors are temporarily supplied while sun.io
65       * converters co-exist with the sun.nio.cs.{ext} charset coders
66       * These facilitate sharing of conversion tables between the
67       * two co-existing implementations. When sun.io converters
68       * are made extinct these will be unncessary and should be removed
69       */
70  
71      public String getDecoderByteToCharMappings() {
72          return Decoder.singleByteToChar;
73      }
74  
75      public short[] getDecoderIndex1() {
76          return Decoder.index1;
77  
78      }
79      public String getDecoderIndex2() {
80          return Decoder.index2;
81  
82      }
83      public short[] getEncoderIndex1() {
84          return Encoder.index1;
85  
86      }
87      public String getEncoderIndex2() {
88          return Encoder.index2;
89  
90      }
91      public String getEncoderIndex2a() {
92          return Encoder.index2a;
93  
94      }
95  
96      protected static class Decoder extends DBCS_IBM_EBCDIC_Decoder {
97  
98          public Decoder(Charset cs) {
99                  super(cs);
100                 super.mask1 = 0xFFC0;
101                 super.mask2 = 0x003F;
102                 super.shift = 6;
103                 super.singleByteToChar = this.singleByteToChar;
104                 super.index1 = this.index1;
105                 super.index2 = this.index2;
106         }
107

1293             super.index2 = index2;
